                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">ذ</orth>
                  </form>, (S, M, A, Mgh, Msb, K,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">إِسْرَارٌ</foreign>; (Msb;) [and accord. to the TA <foreign lang="ar">سَرَّهُ</foreign>; but see the first sentence of this art.;] <hi rend="ital">He concealed it; suppressed it; kept it secret;</hi> (S, M, A, Mgh, Msb, K;) namely, a story, or the like: (A, Mgh, Msb:) and, contr., <hi rend="ital">he manifested it; revealed it; published it; made it known.</hi> (S, M, Msb, K.) Both of these significations have been assigned to the verb in the phrase <foreign lang="ar">وَأَسَرُّوا ٱلنَّدَامَةَ</foreign>, in the Kur [x. 55 and xxxiv. 32]: (S:) some say, that the meaning is <hi rend="ital">They will manifest repentance:</hi> Th says, <hi rend="ital">they will conceal it</hi> from their chiefs: the former [says ISd] is the more correct: (M:) the former meaning is also given on the authority of AO; but Sh says, I have not heard it on the authority of any other; and Az says that the lexicologists most strongly disapprove of the saying of AO; and it is said that the meaning is, <hi rend="ital">they,</hi> the chiefs of the polytheists, <hi rend="ital">will conceal repentance</hi> from the lower class of their people, whom they shall have caused to err; and in like manner say Zj and the [other] expositors. (TA.) In like manner also the two contr. significations are assigned to the verb in the saying of Imra-el- Keys, [in his Mo'allakah,] <foreign lang="ar">لَوْ يُسِرُّونَ مَقْتَلِى</foreign>, which As used to quote with <foreign lang="ar">ش</foreign>, thus, <foreign lang="ar">لَوْ يُشِرُّونَ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">مَقْتَلِى</foreign>, meaning <hi rend="ital">that they might publish,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">make known, my slaughter.</hi> (S.) You say also, <foreign lang="ar">أَسَرَّ إِلَيْهِ حَدِيثًا</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">He revealed unto him a story</hi> (S, K) <hi rend="ital">secretly.</hi> (TA.) An ex. occurs in the Kur lxvi. 3. (TA.) And <foreign lang="ar">أَسْرَرْتُ إِلَيْهِ المَوَدَّةَ</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">بِالمَوَدَّةِ</foreign>, <hi rend="ital">I showed,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">manifested, to him love, or affection.</hi> (S.) It is said in the Kur [lx. 1], <foreign lang="ar">تُسِرُّونَ إِلَيْهِمْ بِٱلْمَوَدَّةِ</foreign>, meaning, <hi rend="ital">Ye reveal to them</hi> the news of the Prophet <hi rend="ital">by reason of</hi> the <hi rend="ital">love</hi> that is between you and them; the objective complement of the verb being suppressed: or <foreign lang="ar">المودّة</foreign> may be an objective complement, the <foreign lang="ar">ب</foreign> being a redundant corroborative, as in <foreign lang="ar">أَخَذَ الخِطَامَ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">أَخَذَ بِهِ</foreign>: (Msb:) and this interpretation is correct; for <foreign lang="ar">إِسْرَارٌ</foreign> to a person necessarily implies revealing a secret to him and at the same time concealing it from another. (B.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">وَأَسَرُّوهُ بِضَاعَةً</foreign>, in the Kur xii. 19, signifies <hi rend="ital">And they concealed,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">kept secret, his case,</hi> making him <hi rend="ital">as an article of merchandise:</hi> (Jel:) or <hi rend="ital">they conjectured in their minds that they should obtain, by selling him, merchandise.</hi> (TA.) [See also an ex. voce <foreign lang="ar">اِرْتَغَى</foreign>, in art. <foreign lang="ar">رغو</foreign>.]          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">اسرّ الفَاتِحَةَ</foreign>, and <foreign lang="ar">بِالفَاتِحَةِ</foreign>, <hi rend="ital">He recited the Fátihah</hi> [or First Chapter of the Kur-án] <hi rend="ital">secretly,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">inaudibly:</hi> (Msb:) or the latter form of expression is a mistake. (Mgh.)          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">أَسْرَرْتُهُ</foreign> also signifies <foreign lang="ar">نَسَبْتُهُ إِلَى السِّرِّ</foreign> [which may mean either <hi rend="ital">I attributed it to secrecy,</hi> or, like many phrases of this kind, by inversion, <hi rend="ital">I attributed to him secrecy, or mystery</hi>].
